We used this hotel as the hotel were all our wedding guests were asked to stay, and as the bride and groom we also stayed here. We offered to buy out all the rooms of the hotel, and the manager, Stephanie told us that it would be more economical for each guest or couple to book their own rooms. When we asked our guests to do that, as reservations started trickling in, their website algorithm automatically raised the prices of the remaining rooms since we were creating high demand for that specific weekend. The lowest tiered rooms were three times the price that they originally were, based on the demand we created. When asking the hotel to reduce the price back to the origional price so that our guests can book out the remaining rooms, Stephanie refused and put a note on my account so that anyone I spoke to was aware that they should deny my request. They were elitists and said that they would get the business even if we don't buy out their rooms, so they weren't worried about accommodating our request. It was a terrible experience, and I would never recommend this place for wedding parties. I was planning an entire wedding and having to deal with the staff at this hotel causing me stress. The few guests that got stuck booking a but later, had to look at other hotels because Wine Country Inn refused to bring the price down. When I asked a staff at the hotel to escalate the issue to the owner or manager's manager, he said "you definitely don't want to deal with him". Sounds like they are all under a strict regime!</text>

< username>
Austin Barrett<//username>
< review>
Great location! Quiet and accommodating not far from the road (but you can't hear it whatsoever!). Five stars is near impossible, but it comes quite close at 4.5 stars for us.

Staying in the vineyard view cottage king. The suite is quiet and cozy and shares no walls with any neighbors, with a fun private patio, electric awning, fountain, a roomy bathroom with a jet tub for two, and three shower heads in a nice walk-in shower with a stone bench. Room service options include charcuterie and an assortment of wine (of course). The staff is fantastic, and did my favorite thing of being happily helpful when asked, but otherwise leave you to enjoy yourself. Breakfast was tasty, and they didn't mind we were a little late to the party after a long drive and nighttime arrival.

The fridge is wobbly, but quiet and functional. The fireplace isn't consistent in ours (leaving that thing turned off). The switches are a bit dated, but are dimmable. The bathroom is segmented by high glass walls, but otherwise is sectioned off by just a single door from the rest of the suite. Everything is very well maintained, ventilated, and clean, though. The HVAC, water pressure, and water heater all function perfectly, even down to the heated floors in the bathroom. Bravo.

Recommended for sure, and the price was reasonable as well!</review>

This is a very quaint hotel. I dont know the history but it appears to be a converted farm house or estate manor.  It is a bed and Breakfast type of layout that has cottages also.  This hotel is located near a number of excellent wineries. The rooms are very modern with nice carpeting and flooring throughout. The bathroom is also very modern with marble and glass. Our suite had an outdoor patio area for sitting. The grounds are nice to walk on. They have a heated swimming pool. The room had a small refrigerator and we received a small complimentary bottle of wine. Breakfast is provided in a patio and family room type of setting.   There are many options available for your breakfast enjoyment.  The room was very quiet and had a sitting area along with a 40+ inch television. All in all this was a very nice relaxing environment for a couples experience.</Review>

< Review>
When we arrived at Wine Country Inn & Cottages, our first thought was "this is cute!" We got checked in promptly, set our things down in our amazing room, then went to enjoy the complimentary wine tasting in the lobby (which is apparently limited to just a few weeks).

Unfortunately, the beautiful view from the room and great service from the staff was spoiled by the paper thin walls, and all of the noise that permeated them. All night and morning, we could hear EVERYTHING; people talking above us, every door closing, every footstep taken to a neighboring room. We were able to ignore it for most of the night, but were afraid to get too intimate in fear of neighbors hearing us as clearly as we could hear others.

The worst came at 5am, when one of our upstairs neighbors were up talking and moving about (for some reason). My girlfriend and I both had a really tough time staying asleep with all of the noise.

We took this little vacation to evade the noise that we typically hear around our apartment at home, but unfortunately, even our apartment was quieter than staying in this room.

Other than the noise, the location was great as well. Parking was abundant and we were about 5‚Äì10 minutes away from most wineries and downtown St. Helena, which made grabbing food or a glass of wine easy.

All in all, the experience at Wine Country Inn was pleasant, but due to the rough night of sleep alone, I doubt we'll come back.<//Review>

< Review>
So I‚Äôm not a big review writer but I felt compelled to share about this amazing place. We were on our honeymoon and decided to make a side track to Napa Valley. We found this Inn on yelp and decided to see if they had rooms available.  They did we stayed in there King Junior Suite for a week day we got a discount a killer deal, and the room turned out amazing. Huge king bed, cute sitting room with a fireplace (logs included) huge bathroom with a jetted tub and duel showers and a private patio that over looks the Duckhorn Vineyard.

The staff are the most friendly and sweet people you‚Äôll meet. They truly try to go out of there way to make you feel at home. Complimentary waters and sodas in the room and each has a small bottle of wine waiting for you so you can start your visit off right.

Close to the city less than 5 min drive to the heart of St Helena. Has a pool and hot tube set away from the rooms so you don‚Äôt hear the noise. Tasty continental breakfast included. And as a bonus on Friday and Saturdays they have one of the wineries come in and do a tasting with some gourmet cheese and fruits.

Seriously best place we stayed the whole trip would recommend to anyone looking.< /Review>

From the moment we stepped foot inside we were excited to try out the food. Caroline was sweet and attentive, she explained the menu and was very helpful as well. My husband and I ended up ordering a pepperoni pizza, meatball sandwich, antipasto salad and a large drink.

Antonious Pizza Riverside

I always come to this spot whenever I'm visiting the Mission Inn or checking out various events in the downtown area. Normally, I just get a scoop of ice cream (pistachio is by far the best flavor) and I am always met with excellent service, however I finally got the chance to actually dine here with a friend.¬†‚Ä®‚Ä®It's foolish to ask a Vegan person to come to a pizza restaurant but there are still a few options to go with. On this particular trip I decided to go vegetarian instead and tried their veggie sandwich which included a medley of veggies topped with mustard in a French roll.¬†‚Ä®‚Ä®The food was delicious but if there is one thing that stands out about this place it is their customer service. Every worker I have had the pleasure of talking to has always been a great mix of fun and helpful and if that's not something to make you come back, then perhaps the relatively low cost of their amazing food will!< /text>

<user_name>Jason Lum</user_name><Pics>None</Pics>< resp>
None</resp>
< Text>
It is very difficult to find good pho these days. There's no shortage of pho locations, but even the top place tend to slip. If you want a pretty good pho place without the crazy wait, Pho Ha Noi is for you. Especially you live near by, the other Irvine pho places are not the worth the drive and wait.

It's nice to get the same friendly service every time that I go. I'm guessing that it's family owned and nothing taste better than family made pho. It's easy to love a place when you can build a repore with the staff.

The food here is very basic- nothing fancy, but I like that. They do use MSG, but it doesn't seem to over power the taste of the food. I like the pork chops and rare steak pho. It won't win any awards, but if I'm hungry and don't feel like waiting this place isn't busy most of the time. I've gone here during busier dinner times, but I usually get my food quickly. You won't see the normal Vietnamese people talking loudly to each other because they don't want to work. You have to go else where if you want to experience that.

Food when you want it and it's not fast food. Try Pho Ha Noi!</Text>

<text>The best barbers in The East Bay since 2010. Family friendly, children's haircuts, women's styles, hipster beard manicuring, they do it all here.

They always have 3-5 guys who cut any kind of hair and literally all of them are skilled to do your hair cut, no matter how particular it is. I'm particular about my hair: every barber here has nailed it, every single time.

No rush, or in a rush: they accommodate it all.

Also available by appointment any day of the year!

If you or anyone you know needs a haircut: The Cutz Barbershop in front of Chabot College and next to Smokey's Smoke Shop is the only place to go.

You'll finally feel that the price for a haircut was really worth it with The Cutz.

The Cutz Barbershop is hands down better than SuperCuts, Great Clips, etc., etc. These guys perform haircuts with all the bells and whistles. They don't cut corners here, just any hair that needs cutting.

Don't waste your time or money at any other shop. Save your self the embarrassment of having to grow out a failed haircut.

Get your hair cut, here, at The Cutz Barbershop today!
